FE CIVIL EXAM PREP — BONUS 3 WEB APP

1. A simply supported beam has a span length of 10 meters and carries a uniformly distributed load of 5 kN/m. What is the maximum bending moment in the beam?
   A) 125 kNm
   B) 250 kNm
   C) 300 kNm
   D) 500 kNm

2. An engineer discovers a flaw in a completed project. According to engineering ethics, what should the engineer do first?
   A) Notify the relevant authorities immediately.
   B) Consult the client and propose a solution.
   C) Ignore the issue since the project is complete.
   D) Contact a lawyer for legal protection.

3. What is the future worth of $10,000 after 5 years if the annual interest rate is 6% compounded annually?
   A) $11,337
   B) $13,382
   C) $14,050
   D) $15,000

4. A 3-meter-long uniform beam weighs 300 N and is supported at both ends. A 500 N load is placed 1 meter from the left support. What is the reaction force at the right support?
   A) 400 N
   B) 500 N
   C) 600 N
   D) 700 N

5. A car accelerates uniformly from rest to a speed of 20 m/s in 5 seconds. What is the acceleration of the car?
   A) 2 m/s²
   B) 4 m/s²
   C) 5 m/s²
   D) 10 m/s²

6. What is the derivative of f(x) = 3x² + 5x - 7?
   A) 6x + 5
   B) 3x + 5
   C) 6x - 7
   D) 3x²

7. An engineer is asked to approve a design they did not work on or review. What is the ethical action to take?
   A) Approve the design to save time.
   B) Request sufficient time to review the design.
   C) Refuse to approve the design under any circumstances.
   D) Approve the design but note the lack of review.

8. What is the present worth of $1,000 to be received 5 years from now if the interest rate is 8% annually?
   A) $680.58
   B) $735.03
   C) $900.00
   D) $1,080.00

9. A 4-meter-long beam is simply supported at both ends and carries a point load of 500 N at the center. What is the reaction force at one of the supports?
   A) 500 N
   B) 250 N
   C) 1000 N
   D) 0 N

10. A 2 kg object moves in a circular path with a radius of 3 meters at a constant speed of 4 m/s. What is the centripetal force acting on the object?
   A) 8 N
   B) 10.67 N
   C) 12 N
   D) 16 N

11. A steel rod with a cross-sectional area of 0.01 m² is subjected to a tensile force of 50 kN. What is the stress in the rod?
   A) 50 MPa
   B) 5 kPa
   C) 500 kPa
   D) 5 MPa

12. Which material property measures the ability to resist deformation under load?
   A) Ductility
   B) Elastic Modulus
   C) Toughness
   D) Hardness

13. What is the Reynold's number for water flowing at a velocity of 2 m/s in a pipe with a diameter of 0.1 m? Assume kinematic viscosity = 1×10⁻⁶ m²/s.
   A) 20,000
   B) 10,000
   C) 5,000
   D) 2,000

14. How many degrees are in a bearing of N45°E?
   A) 45°
   B) 90°
   C) 135°
   D) 180°

15. What is the primary purpose of a detention basin in stormwater management?
   A) Filter pollutants
   B) Reduce peak discharge rates
   C) Increase groundwater recharge
   D) Provide water for irrigation

16. What is the integral of f(x) = 5x^4 + 3x^2 with respect to x?
   A) x^5 + x^3 + C
   B) x^5 + x^3 + 7
   C) x^5 + 3x^3 + C
   D) (5/5)x^5 + (3/3)x^3 + C

17. An engineer encounters a design flaw that could compromise safety. What is the most ethical course of action?
   A) Ignore the flaw and proceed with the project.
   B) Report the flaw to the relevant stakeholders and suggest corrective measures.
   C) Fix the issue without informing anyone.
   D) Delay the project until someone else notices the flaw.

   A) $6,200
   B) $6,349.92
   C) $6,480
   D) $6,509.36

   A) Ceramic

   D) y = x^2 + 4

--- CORRECT ANSWERS AND EXPLANATIONS ---

1. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The maximum bending moment for a simply supported beam with a uniform load is given by M = wL^2/8. Substituting w = 5 kN/m and L = 10 m, M = (5 * 10^2) / 8 = 125 kNm.

2. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Engineering ethics requires engineers to prioritize public safety and inform the client of any issues while suggesting solutions.

3. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Future worth is calculated using F = P(1 + i)^n. Here, P = $10,000, i = 0.06, n = 5. F = 10,000(1 + 0.06)^5 = $14,050.

4. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Using the equation of equilibrium for moments about the left support: (500 * 1) + (300 * 1.5) = R2 * 3, solving gives R2 = 400 N.

5. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Acceleration is given by a = (v - u)/t. Here, u = 0, v = 20 m/s, t = 5 s. a = (20 - 0)/5 = 4 m/s².

6. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The derivative of 3x² is 6x, the derivative of 5x is 5, and the constant -7 becomes 0.

7. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: According to engineering ethics, designs should only be approved after proper review.

8. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Present Worth = Future Value / (1 + interest rate)^years = 1000 / (1 + 0.08)^5.

9. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The load is symmetrically distributed, so each support carries half of the load: 500 N / 2 = 250 N.

10. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: Centripetal Force = (mass × velocity²) / radius = (2 × 4²) / 3 = 16 N.

11. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Stress = Force / Area = 50,000 N / 0.01 m² = 50 × 10⁶ N/m² = 50 MPa.

12. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Elastic modulus quantifies a material's ability to resist elastic deformation under load.

13. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Re = (Velocity × Diameter) / Kinematic Viscosity = (2 × 0.1) / 1×10⁻⁶ = 20,000.

14. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: A bearing of N45°E specifies a 45° angle measured clockwise from the north direction.

15. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Detention basins are designed to temporarily store stormwater to reduce peak discharge rates.

16. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The integral of 5x^4 is (5/5)x^5 and the integral of 3x^2 is (3/3)x^3. Add the constant of integration, C.

17. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: According to engineering ethics, safety is paramount, and reporting any potential issues is essential for transparency and resolution.

18. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: Use the compound interest formula: FV = PV(1 + i)^n. Here, FV = 5000(1 + 0.08)^3 = $6,509.36.

19. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: For equilibrium, the pin and roller share the load equally. Each reaction force is 10 kN / 2 = 5 kN.

20. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Kinetic energy is given by KE = 0.5 * m * v^2. Substituting, KE = 0.5 * 2 * (10)^2 = 200 J.

21. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Stress = Force / Area. The area of the bar is πd²/4 = π(0.02)²/4. Stress = 10,000 / Area = 31.8 MPa.

22. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Mild steel is known for its ductility, allowing it to deform significantly before fracturing.

23. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Volumetric flow rate = Area * Velocity. Area = πd²/4 = π(0.3)²/4. Q = 0.36 m³/s.

24. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Horizontal displacement = 500 + 300cos(30°). The result is approximately 800 m.

25. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Sedimentation basins allow solid particles to settle out of water due to gravity.

26. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The integral of 3x^2 is x^3, and adding the constant of integration C, we use the initial condition y(0)=4 to find C=4.

27. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Engineers must prioritize public safety and report unsafe conditions to the responsible party promptly.

28. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Using the Annual Worth method, subtract the cost per year from the annual return at the given interest rate.

29. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The reaction moment is calculated as force × distance from the fixed end: 500 N × 3 m = 1500 Nm.

30. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Momentum is calculated as mass × velocity: 10 kg × 15 m/s = 150 kg·m/s.

31. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Stress is force divided by area: 100,000 N / 0.005 m² = 200 MPa.

32. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Ductile materials undergo significant plastic deformation before breaking.

33. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Volumetric flow rate is area × velocity. Area = π(0.2/2)², Q = A × 3 m/s.

34. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Horizontal distance is calculated using the cosine of the slope angle.

35. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Retention basins are designed to store water temporarily to reduce peak runoff.

36. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Axial stress = force / area = 200,000 N / 0.01 m² = 20 MPa.

37. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The integral is computed by increasing the power of each term by 1 and dividing by that new power.

38. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Ethical guidelines require engineers to prioritize safety and public welfare over deadlines or client preferences.

39. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The future worth is calculated using the formula F = P(1 + i)^n, where P is the present value, i is the interest rate, and n is the number of years.

40. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The total load is 50 kN, which is equally distributed to the two supports due to symmetry.

41. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Acceleration is calculated as the change in velocity divided by time: (30 - 10) / 5 = 2 m/s².

42. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Stress is calculated as force divided by area: 100,000 N / 0.01 m² = 100 MPa.

43. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: Modulus of Elasticity measures a material's resistance to deformation under applied stress.

44. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Reynolds number is calculated as Re = (velocity × diameter) / kinematic viscosity.

   Explanation: A bearing is measured clockwise from the north; due east corresponds to 90°.

   Explanation: Sedimentation basins are designed to remove suspended solids from water through gravitational settling.

47. Correct Answer: A

   Explanation: The NSPE Code of Ethics prohibits engineers from accepting gifts that could create a conflict of interest.

   Explanation: Using the formula for annual worth: AW = (P * A/P) - (S * A/F), the result is $7,072.80.

   Explanation: In a simply supported beam with a centered point load, each support shares half the load.

51. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: Kinetic energy is calculated using KE = 0.5 * m * v^2. Substituting the values gives KE = 0.5 * 5 * (8^2) = 160 J.

   Explanation: Reynolds number is calculated using Re = (ρVD)/μ or Re = (VD)/ν. Re = (3 * 0.2) / (1.004 x 10^-6) = 597,000.

   Explanation: Use the Pythagorean theorem: d = √(200² + 300²) = √(40000 + 90000) = 500 m.

   Explanation: An aeration tank introduces oxygen to promote biological treatment by microorganisms.

   Explanation: The integral ∫(2x^3 + 3x - 5)dx evaluates to (1/2)x^4 + (3/2)x^2 - 5x. Substituting the limits 0 to 2 gives the result 14.

   Explanation: An engineer should not approve documents for which they lack sufficient knowledge, as per professional ethics.

67. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The definite integral of 3x^2 + 2x - 5 from 1 to 3 is calculated as [(x^3 + x^2 - 5x) at x=3] - [(x^3 + x^2 - 5x) at x=1], which gives 24.

   Explanation: The NSPE Code of Ethics requires engineers to avoid circumstances that could compromise their integrity or appear as a conflict of interest.

71. Correct Answer: D
